[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **What happened**  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running the fuzz target `avif_fuzztest_yuvrgb@YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reported a “dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow” in [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow`. The overflow occurs when reading four bytes from a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack buffer beyond its intended bounds.[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  A stack-based buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdynamic-stack-buffer-overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where a read [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation exceeds the allocated stack frame.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash trace pinpoints the exact location:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/reformat.c around line [0m[1;36m797[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m812[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, two VLAs [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mheight[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and `vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mheight[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` are indexed at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi + a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj + b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` without any bounds checking on `i + a` or `j + b`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `i` or `j` sits at a border [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m or width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m/height-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `a` or `b` equals[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m±[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,  [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     the code reads or writes beyond the stack-allocated array, triggering a stack [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer overflow.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Introduce explicit clamping of the dampening offsets so that the adjusted [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindices  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      always lie within valid [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, width–[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m and [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, height–[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compute signed loop coordinates before applying `a`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`b`:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int ii = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int jj = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int ai = ii + a;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int bj = jj + b;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m clamp to valid range[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if      [0m[1;39m([0m[39mai <  [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m           ai = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mai >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  ai = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if      [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbj <  [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m           bj = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbj >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m bj = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Replace all direct accesses `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mai[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mbj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and `vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mai[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mbj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach follows the same “clamp to edge” logic already used elsewhere in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreprojection code paths,  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     preserving the overall spill-dampening effect for border pixels while [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing out-of-bounds.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other control flow, calculations of `total_spill`, and loop boundaries [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain unchanged.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/reformat.c` and locate `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` around line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m797[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. After determining `a` and `b`, insert the signed-index calculation and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclamping snippet [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee [0m[1;36m2.[0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace subsequent `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and `vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences with the clamped indices.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun libFuzzer’s `YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert` to confirm the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer error no longer reproduces.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigations:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only change is to enforce valid indexing; spill values from immediate [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneighbors on borders remain defined.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance impact is negligible [0m[1;39m([0m[39msmall integer ops per pixel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No tests or harness code are modified; existing GTest suites and fuzz targets [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to operate identically.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar Pattern in Codebase:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Upstream in the same file, adjacent-pixel sampling already clamps out-of-range[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcoordinates for chroma up/downsampling.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch harmonizes dampening logic with those existing safety measures.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:790[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m820[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
